[2025-03-19 07:51:35] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => 
            SELECT 
                e.id,
                u.username as student,
                u.email,
                c.title as course,
                e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date,
                e.status
            FROM enrollments e
            LEFT JOIN users u ON e.student_id = u.id
            LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id
            WHERE 1=1
         AND e.enrollment_date >= :date_from AND e.enrollment_date <= :date_to ORDER BY e.enrollment_date DESC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [:date_from] => 2025-02-19
            [:date_to] => 2025-03-19 23:59:59
        )

)

[2025-03-19 07:52:55] Assignment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT a.id, (SELECT title FROM courses WHERE id = a.course_id) as course, a.title as assignment, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id) as submissions, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id AND s.grade IS NOT NULL) as graded, COALESCE((SELECT ROUND(AVG(s.grade), 2) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id AND s.grade IS NOT NULL), 0) as avg_grade, a.due_date FROM assignments a WHERE 1=1 ORDER BY a.due_date DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

[2025-03-19 07:53:05] Generating performance report: Array
(
    [courseId] => all
    [period] => last_month
)

[2025-03-19 07:53:05] Performance report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => 
            SELECT 
                c.id,
                c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id AND e.status = 'active') as active_students,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id AND e.status = 'completed') as completion_count,
                CASE 
                    WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) > 0 
                    THEN ROUND((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id AND e.status = 'completed') * 100.0 / 
                        (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id), 2) || '%'
                    ELSE '0%'
                END as completion_rate,
            c.start_date,
            c.end_date
            FROM courses c
            WHERE 1=1 AND c.created_at >= date('now', '-1 month') ORDER BY c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

[2025-03-19 07:57:13] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => 
            SELECT 
                u.id,
                u.username as teacher,
                u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM assignments a WHERE a.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count
            FROM users u
            WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19

[2025-03-19 08:02:54] Assignment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT a.id, (SELECT title FROM courses WHERE id = a.course_id) as course, a.title as assignment, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id) as submissions, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id AND s.grade IS NOT NULL) as graded, COALESCE((SELECT ROUND(AVG(s.grade), 2) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id AND s.grade IS NOT NULL), 0) as avg_grade, a.due_date FROM assignments a WHERE 1=1 ORDER BY a.due_date DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

(
    [query] => SELECT e.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, 'Unknown' as status FROM enrollments e LEFT JOIN users u ON e.student_id = u.id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE 1=1 AND e.enrollment_date >= :date_from AND e.enrollment_date <= :date_to ORDER BY e.enrollment_date DESC, e.id DESC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all

[2025-03-19 08:11:02] Assignments table has teacher_id column: 
[2025-03-19 08:11:02] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-19 08:11:02] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => 
            SELECT 
                u.id,
                u.username as teacher,
                u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count
            FROM users u
            WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
)

    [count] => 5

[2025-03-19 08:11:34] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => 
            SELECT 
                u.id,
                u.username as teacher,
                u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count
            FROM users u
            WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
)

    [courseId] => all

                c.id,

            c.end_date
            FROM courses c

[2025-03-19 08:16:10] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' AND (e.enrollment_date >= :date_from OR e.id IS NULL) AND (e.enrollment_date <= :date_to OR e.id IS NULL) ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
            [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
        )

)

    [query] => 
            SELECT 
                c.id,
                c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate,
            c.start_date,
            c.end_date
            FROM courses c
            WHERE 1=1 AND c.created_at >= date('now', '-1 month') ORDER BY c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all

[2025-03-19 08:17:57] Assignments table has teacher_id column: 
[2025-03-19 08:17:57] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-19 08:17:57] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => 
            SELECT 
                u.id,
                u.username as teacher,
                u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count
            FROM users u
            WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
)

(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19

[2025-03-19 08:20:57] Assignment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT a.id, (SELECT title FROM courses WHERE id = a.course_id) as course, a.title as assignment, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id) as submissions, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id AND s.grade IS NOT NULL) as graded, COALESCE((SELECT ROUND(AVG(s.grade), 2) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id AND s.grade IS NOT NULL), 0) as avg_grade, a.due_date, CASE 
                WHEN a.due_date < date('now') THEN 'Past Due'
                WHEN a.due_date >= date('now') THEN 'Open'
                ELSE 'Unknown'
            END as status FROM assignments a WHERE 1=1 ORDER BY a.due_date DESC, a.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
    [status] => all
)

[2025-03-19 08:23:15] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' AND (e.enrollment_date >= :date_from OR e.id IS NULL) AND (e.enrollment_date <= :date_to OR e.id IS NULL) ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
            [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
        )

[2025-03-19 08:24:07] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-19 08:24:07] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
)

    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' AND (e.enrollment_date >= :date_from OR e.id IS NULL) AND (e.enrollment_date <= :date_to OR e.id IS NULL) ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
            [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
        )

)

[2025-03-19 08:24:18] Assignment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT a.id, (SELECT title FROM courses WHERE id = a.course_id) as course, a.title as assignment, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id) as submissions, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id AND s.grade IS NOT NULL) as graded, COALESCE((SELECT ROUND(AVG(s.grade), 2) FROM submissions s WHERE s.assignment_id = a.id AND s.grade IS NOT NULL), 0) as avg_grade, a.due_date, CASE 
                WHEN a.due_date < date('now') THEN 'Past Due'
                WHEN a.due_date >= date('now') THEN 'Open'
                ELSE 'Unknown'
            END as status FROM assignments a WHERE 1=1 ORDER BY a.due_date DESC, a.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
    [status] => all
)

[2025-03-19 08:25:21] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-19 08:25:21] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
)

[2025-03-19 08:25:27] Performance report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT c.id, c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate, c.start_date, c.end_date, c.status FROM courses c WHERE 1=1 AND c.created_at >= date('now', '-1 month') ORDER BY c.created_at DESC, c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' AND (e.enrollment_date >= :date_from OR e.id IS NULL) AND (e.enrollment_date <= :date_to OR e.id IS NULL) ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
            [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
        )

)

[2025-03-19 08:37:18] Performance report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT c.id, c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate, c.start_date, c.end_date, c.status FROM courses c WHERE 1=1 AND c.created_at >= date('now', '-1 month') ORDER BY c.created_at DESC, c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

[2025-03-19 08:37:23] Assignments table has teacher_id column: 
[2025-03-19 08:37:23] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-19 08:37:23] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
)

[2025-03-19 17:13:31] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
)

(
    [query] => SELECT c.id, c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate, c.start_date, c.end_date, c.status FROM courses c WHERE 1=1 AND c.created_at >= date('now', '-1 month') ORDER BY c.created_at DESC, c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all

[2025-03-19 17:13:59] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' AND (e.enrollment_date >= :date_from OR e.id IS NULL) AND (e.enrollment_date <= :date_to OR e.id IS NULL) ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 2025-02-19
            [dateTo] => 2025-03-19
        )

)

                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,

    [courseId] => all

[2025-03-20 06:19:33] Assignments table has teacher_id column: 
[2025-03-20 06:19:33] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-20 06:19:33] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE teacher_id = u.id AND created_at >= :date_from AND created_at <= :date_to AND status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 2025-02-20
    [dateTo] => 2025-03-20
)

[2025-03-20 06:28:40] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' AND (e.enrollment_date >= :date_from OR e.id IS NULL) AND (e.enrollment_date <= :date_to OR e.id IS NULL) ORDER BY u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 2025-02-20
            [dateTo] => 2025-03-20
        )

[2025-03-20 06:33:22] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' AND (e.enrollment_date >= :date_from OR e.id IS NULL) AND (e.enrollment_date <= :date_to OR e.id IS NULL) ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 2025-02-20
            [dateTo] => 2025-03-20
        )

)

(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array

[2025-03-20 07:11:04] Performance report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT c.id, c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate, c.start_date, c.end_date, c.status FROM courses c WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY c.created_at DESC, c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

[2025-03-20 07:11:09] Assignments table has teacher_id column: 
[2025-03-20 07:11:09] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-20 07:11:09] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id AND c.status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 
    [dateTo] => 
)

[2025-03-21 06:27:34] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-21 06:27:34] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id AND c.status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 
    [dateTo] => 
)

[2025-03-21 06:27:34] Teacher report results: Array
(

[2025-03-21 07:01:16] Performance report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT c.id, c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate, c.start_date, c.end_date, c.status FROM courses c WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY c.created_at DESC, c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

[2025-03-21 07:01:21] Performance report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT c.id, c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate, c.start_date, c.end_date, c.status FROM courses c WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY c.created_at DESC, c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

[2025-03-21 07:01:24] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id AND c.status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 
    [dateTo] => 
)

[2025-03-21 09:00:08] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 
            [dateTo] => 
        )

)

[2025-03-21 19:04:28] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 
            [dateTo] => 
        )

[2025-03-21 19:07:49] Assignments table has teacher_id column: 
[2025-03-21 19:07:49] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-03-21 19:07:49] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id AND c.status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 
    [dateTo] => 
)

(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array

[2025-04-01 08:57:10] Performance report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT c.id, c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate, c.start_date, c.end_date, c.status FROM courses c WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY c.created_at DESC, c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all
)

[2025-04-01 13:41:41] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-04-01 13:41:41] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id AND c.status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 
    [dateTo] => 
)

                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,

[2025-04-01 13:45:27] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id AND c.status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 
    [dateTo] => 
)

[2025-04-02 03:00:40] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all
            [dateFrom] => 
            [dateTo] => 
        )

)

(
    [query] => SELECT c.id, c.title as course,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as enrollments,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM enrollments e WHERE e.course_id = c.id) as active_students,
                    0 as completion_count,
                    '0%' as completion_rate, c.start_date, c.end_date, c.status FROM courses c WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY c.created_at DESC, c.id DESC
    [courseId] => all

[2025-04-02 05:33:49] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-04-02 05:33:49] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id AND c.status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 
    [dateTo] => 
)

[2025-04-02 05:48:27] Assignments table has teacher_id column: 
[2025-04-02 05:48:27] Course assignments table exists: 1
[2025-04-02 05:48:27] Teacher report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as teacher, u.email,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as courses_created,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id AND c.status = 'active') as active_courses,
                (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                 FROM course_assignments ca 
                 JOIN courses c ON ca.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as assignments_created,
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.student_id) 
                 FROM enrollments e 
                 JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id 
                 WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) as students_count, CASE 
                WHEN (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM courses c WHERE c.teacher_id = u.id) > 0 THEN 'Active' 
                ELSE 'Inactive' 
            END as status FROM users u WHERE u.role = 'teacher' ORDER BY u.created_at DESC, u.id DESC
    [teacherId] => all
    [dateFrom] => 
    [dateTo] => 
)

[2025-04-02 05:50:17] Enrollment report SQL: Array
(
    [query] => SELECT u.id, u.username as student, u.email, c.title as course, e.enrollment_date as enrolled_date, CASE WHEN e.id IS NULL THEN 'Not Enrolled' ELSE 'Enrolled' END as status FROM users u LEFT JOIN enrollments e ON u.id = e.student_id LEFT JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id WHERE u.role = 'student' ORDER BY CASE WHEN e.enrollment_date IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, e.enrollment_date DESC, u.username ASC
    [params] => Array
        (
            [courseId] => all

            [dateTo] =>
